## Page 2

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">内</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">容</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">简</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">介</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">本书主要描述</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 系统的总体框架和设计思想，包含很多可以直接操作的实例。编写本书的目的是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">希望读者对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">系统背后的逻辑有一个全面的了解。本书对比较核心且常用的技术点有更加深入的解释，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">对实际使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 系统工作大有裨益，同时，选择重点的方向进行源码级深度分析，包含大量的案例，而</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">且增加了与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 同类操作系统的对比，涉及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 系统的一些实现，对操作系统的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">描述更清晰。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">本书适合</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 系统开发人员、嵌入式系统开发人员阅读，也可供计算机相关专业的师生阅读。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZHTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 3

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">  </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSJW--GB1-0';font-size:24.00pt;color:#000000">推 荐 序 一 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统在超级计算机、互联网服务、桌面系统、移动和嵌入式设备等领</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">域使用广泛，相关的从业人员和兴趣爱好者一直对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的理论和实践有较大需求。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">本人作为互联网领域的从业人员，非常荣幸可以提前阅读书中的内容。本书内容从</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核层面出发，结合作者多年的实践，对各个子系统的设计、实现和演化进行梳理。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">我认为本书具有以下特点。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第一个特点是解释透彻。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发展至今已经超过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">25</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 年，源代码融合了不同时</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">期的演进和变化，回顾当时的背景，有助于清晰了解源代码作者的意图和目标。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第二个特点是实践性强。在技术领域，实践往往能加深读者对相关概念的理</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">解，本书中的很多案例都可以作为实验，感兴趣的读者可在单机环境或者虚拟机环</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">境完成。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第三个特点是指路明灯。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核的子系统和模块非常多，覆盖的应用范围</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">也很广，面面俱到显然是不现实的。作者希望更多地展示代码背后的思想，以及对</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">其思考后的理解，这比单纯的技术讲解更有营养价值，同时也鼓励读者在阅读时形</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">成自己的见解，学会查阅相关的技术资料。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第四个特点是与时俱进。近几年，业界利用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 构建很多热点应用，本书在</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">很多方面覆盖了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的新功能，对从业者有较大帮助。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p003_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 4

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">总的来讲，本人阅读本书后收获颇丰，对工作也有很大帮助，希望其他读者也</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">能从中获取价值。本人也是一名开源爱好者，感谢作者的辛勤付出，编写出这本内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">容详尽的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 著作，希望</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和其他开源社区发展得越来越好。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSJW--GB1-0';font-size:24.00pt;color:#000000">推 荐 序 二 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在当今移动互联网和人工智能技术快速发展的时代，无论是服务器端程序还是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">智能终端（手机、手表、电视）程序，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统都是主流的操作系统，应用非</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">常广泛。基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核衍生的发行版众多，包括</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">OpenSuse</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RedHat</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CentOS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ubuntu</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等，在如此广泛的应用下，熟悉和理解</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核原理对于广大的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">作系统研发工程师就显得尤为重要。理解</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统内核原理可以帮助操作系统研</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">发工程师在结合</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的系统原理，充分利用操作系统资源和机制的基础上，设计</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">出更稳定、更可靠、更高效的应用程序。同时，学习</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核设计（负载均衡、</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内存管理、网络框架等）可以指导我们设计更复杂的互联网技术架构。本书作者拥</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">有多年的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核研发工作经验，对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核各个模块的原理进行了深入剖析，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">通过畅读本书，我有以下几方面体会。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第一，数据结构和算法解释详尽。数据结构和算法是程序设计和开发的基础，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">本书可以作为参考学习</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核数据结构设计的参考书。比如，第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2.2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 节关于</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核数据结构，链表、哈希表和动态数组等数据结构；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">10</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 章关于路由查找</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的算法、拥塞控制算法和一致性哈希算法等。本书详细介绍了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核的数据结</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">构和算法，同时提供了大量的示例代码。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第二，内核原理和设计剖析透彻。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核有非常多的经典设计，本书都进行</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">了详细解释，非常清晰易懂。比如第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">10</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 章第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">10.4</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 节关于内核网络四层负载均衡架</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">构、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Netfilter</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 过滤框架都是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 经典的技术框架，本书对此剖析得很透彻；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">12</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">章关于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux ELF</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的格式，对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 程序编译、加载和运行的原理，都写得很清晰。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">本书第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 版加入了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与其他操作系统的对比分析，因为不同的操作系统有</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">着不同点和相同点，通过对比分析可以让读者更容易系统理解设计，甚至产生新的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">设计。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">学习</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核最好的方法是阅读源码，但是只看源码往往会无从下手，或者</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">很难理解其中的设计思路。本书与实现方式相结合，对案例所涉及的每个模块都提</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">供了设计思路，可以帮助读者知其然并知其所以然。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">我工作在与内核相关的应用领域，所以，本书的内容都是从实践中提炼出来的，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">希望所提炼的内容能够帮助读者，让读者更好地理解和实现系统设计。如果你是初</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">实践者，希望你能通过内容与我共鸣。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">操作系统总览</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ················································································ 1 </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">12</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">二进制</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ····················································································· 516 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">12.1  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">二进制原理</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ·············································································· 516 </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">12.1.1  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">编译、链接与执行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ································································· 516 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">12.1.2  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">裸程序</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ·············································································· 518 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">12.1.3  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">加载器</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ·············································································· 519 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">12.1.4  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">链接过程</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ··········································································· 523 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">12.2  ELF</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 格式</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ················································································· 525 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">12.2.1  ABI</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ················································································· 525 </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">12.3  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数调用约定</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ··········································································· 547 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">12.4  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">二进制安全</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> ·············································································· 552 </span>

## Page 14

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:25.98pt;color:#000000">第1 章 </span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialBlack';font-size:42.00pt;color:#ffffff">1 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZDBSJW--GB1-0';font-size:25.98pt;color:#000000">操作系统总览 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000">1.1  操作系统简介 </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">操作系统的发展经历了一个百花齐放的过程，现在只剩下少数的几个占据绝对</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">市场统治地位的系统。随着我国经济的发展，国内计算机领域对于操作系统技术的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">需求越来越旺盛。未来，无论操作系统的市场如何变化，其底层所依赖的内核的核</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">心算法原理都不会有太大的变化。各操作系统在调度、内存管理和中断处理这几个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">比较核心的方向都会趋同，这是因为它们都在彼此学习、互相演进。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">人们曾经为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RISC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（精简指令集计算机）和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CISC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（复杂指令集计算机）孰优孰</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">劣吵得不可开交，最后人们发现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Intel</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CISC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 已经吸纳了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RISC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的一些优势技术，</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RISC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也在使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CISC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的某些技术。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">好的信息技术具备极强的传播速度。当前我们熟悉的操作系统有：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HarmonyOS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Mac OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">BSD</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等。在这些操作系统中，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">有些并不只是单纯的操作系统，比如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 实际上也是一个内核。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">21</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 世纪初，操作系统的发展主要是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 不断地从不同的角度发现</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">自身的局限性，并且从各自的角度出发来试图解决这些局限性。在这个发展过程中，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">大量的弥补措施和新机制被发明，但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都要兼容旧的功能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 演进的过程积累了一个很重要的经验是微内核应该怎么设计，“一切皆对</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">象”的思路指导着</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 各个功能的演进；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 演进的过程主要是对服务质量</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p014_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

---

## Page 15

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的优化，“一切皆文件”的思想指导着整个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统的发展。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 擅长的方面，</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也在不断地跟进；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 擅长的方面，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也想与之一较高下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核上市之前出现过很多优秀的内核，直至今日，那些具有竞争关系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的优秀内核仍然存在。比如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">FreeBSD</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Solaris</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 曾经炙手可热，直到现在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">FreeBSD</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">仍然具有强大的生命力。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">直到今天，一个软件想要获得广泛的应用，开源仍旧是很好的方式。软件通过</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">开源的方式能够使取得更大的市场空间，但是代价就是难以找到盈利模式。近年，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">谷歌对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 做了大量的改进和修复，所以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 形成了独特的特点：求稳、求全、</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">争做第一。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是由贝尔实验室开发的操作系统，其设计者阵容可谓豪华：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Rob Pike</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（目</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">前在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Google</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 工作，负责</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言的开发）；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ken Thompson</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 设计者）；</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Dennis Ritchie</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 设计者）；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Brian Kernighan</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">AWK</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 之父）；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Doug Mcilroy</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 管道提出者和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 开发的参与者）。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的本质思想也是“一切皆文件”：</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个文件、内存是一个文件、网络是一个文件，任何东西都是一个文件。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都是多用户分时操作系统，即多个用户共享一个操作系统资源。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">不管是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、内存还是网络，都需要通过调度器来分配、调度。比如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器的文件</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">需要使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来处理，就只能通过某种协议，将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器的文件下载到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">机器中，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器处理完以后再回传到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器中。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的“一切皆文件”看起来</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">很好地解决了这个问题：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器想使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，只需要将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 挂</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">载到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机器的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的文件中就能完成这个需求了。当然，两个机器之间也可以使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">9P</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">”协议来进行文件挂载。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个分布式操作系统，它能把网络上的一切资源都当作文件来使用，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这其实就是云的概念了。但是看起来好的东西在实际使用中不一定好，很多时候人</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">们会更倾向于使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">socket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，就像本可以用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Python</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言的一行代码完成一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">socket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">但是在某些极端情况下还得使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">socket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，因为那样更加可控并且效率高。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进程的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Namespace</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 概念被新晋操作系统</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 几乎完整地继承了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">除</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 之外，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统还有很多重量级的竞争对手：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Haiku</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">BeOS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Amiga</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">OS/2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Arthur</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">XTS-400</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统目前在嵌入式和服务器领域取得了成功，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这两个大方向明显很适合它。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核的第一作者</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linus</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一位有情怀的技术人，他没有选择成立闭源的商</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">业公司，虽然他可能会因此失去一个伟大的公司，但是他却收获了一个伟大的产品，</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p015_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

---

## Page 16

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">并且极大地促进了人类信息技术的进步。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一直都有很多人纠结关于宏内核和微内核的选择。对于公司来说，想要快速产</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">业化，使用微内核几乎是唯一选择。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linus</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 之前，没有人会想到宏内核能成功。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">直到今天，宏内核能走多远也没有人能准确预测。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">微内核是一种社会性的内核，宏内核是一种技术性的内核。在性能方面，微内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">核能击败宏内核的概率不大，因为宏内核中的任何一个细分变更都需要整合测试，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">而且任何一个细分都在整体的框架内变更，包括架构风格和编码风格。但是微内核</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">也有自己不同层面的性能优势。如果</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核采用微内核，其内容又会留下几个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">呢？最后出现的现象很可能是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的一部分代码被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核拿去组建自己的系统，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">另外一部分代码又被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核拿去组建自己的系统。这样的力量分散，很可能无法形</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">成如今的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">几乎可以肯定，任何一个公司在决定创造一个操作系统的时候，最佳选择都是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">使用微内核，且微内核的整体设计可以直接借鉴</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的成功经验，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">设计代表目前商业操作系统的最广泛存在。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">竞争，在本质上是市场壁垒、人员壁垒。正是由于竞争的存在，每一个操作系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统都在痛苦地迭代，各自面临着痛点。操作系统这个领域正在良性地往前发展。我</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">们应该看到的不是各个操作系统之间的区别，而是各个操作系统之间相同的地方。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">例如，对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Cache</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 管理、对调度的公平思路、对中断的处理等，不同的操作系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统在对待这些问题时的处理细节不同，但解决方法是相似的。毕竟，每个操作系统</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要面对的硬件情况基本都是一样的，没有系统可以超脱</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IPI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> （</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Inter-Processor </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Interrupts</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）来设计</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SMP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Symmetric Multiprocessing</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">），也没有系统可以超脱</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">MMU</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">硬件来管理内存（当然</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NO-MMU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的技术一般用于低端嵌入式设备），更没有人可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">x86</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的平台上无视</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">APIC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Advanced Programmable Interrupt Controller</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）来完成中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">断处理。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">操作系统本质上是对市场上已有硬件的适应，适应的程度几乎完全受到硬件市</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">场占有率的影响。反过来，操作系统又会对硬件的发展提出要求。两者相互作用，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在这个过程中，软件与硬件配合的模式会被逐渐固化，最后就变成：操作系统就该</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这么写，因为硬件就是这样的；硬件就该这样，因为操作系统只支持这样的硬件。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统是一个工具、一个平台，也是最近</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">20</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 年对信息产业贡献非常大的开</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">源项目。路由器、手机、监控系统、互联网的服务器，以及桌面系统都在逐渐地应</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统。甚至在很多信息系统里，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统都是唯一的选择。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第1 章 操作系统总览 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p016_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

---

## Page 17

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核比较常用的机制是由用户端底层库进行封装提供的，所以当你需要底</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">层知识时，使用的就是底层库提供的机制，如果底层库提供不了，就由内核直接提</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">供。在通常情况下，底层库都需要尽可能地封装内核提供的功能，但是由于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核的特性是尽可能地集中功能，并且直接通过文件系统暴露接口，这就使得例如</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">/proc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">/dev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等文件系统可以非常方便地直接调用到内核的功能，底层库也就没有必</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要封装了。这里的底层库确切地说是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是内核接口的“产品经理”，其作为</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核对用户空间暴露接口的一个包装，会封装它认为可以更方便用户使用的内核功能。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当我们深入到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 时，通常会同时接触到底层库和内核的用户空间接口。而</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要使用这些底层功能，通常需要对这些功能本身的实现原理有一定的了解。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000">1.2  如何形成一个内核</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核提供的核心功能只有一个——资源管理。资源管理大致分为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 种，即</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">资管调度、内存管理、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 管理。内核中包含了必须要被包含的功能，所谓的“必须</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要被包含的功能”就是频繁需要特权指令运行的内容。可以将偶尔需要用到特权指</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">令运行的功能放到用户态，将拥有特权指令的功能放到内核态。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">所谓操作系统内核，就是多任务彼此安全可靠、高性能运行的一种组织方式。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VxWorks</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（实时操作系统）就是以全内核模式运行所有任务的，因为这个系统的定</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">位就是对所有的任务都高度信任。内核态和用户态的本质区别是，内核态不希望让</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">不可控的用户态的逻辑影响到整个系统的安全性和稳定性。宏内核、微内核和</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VxWorks</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在技术层面其实都是对任务的信任问题的解答。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">无论是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Mac OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">I/O Kit</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，还是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HAL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都试图在开源中撕开一个缺口，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">既希望得到开源的优势，又希望得到企业的支持。因为所有人都不得不面对一个现</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">实：很多硬件企业非常重视自己的设计，认为驱动的暴露会导致设计的泄露，从而</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">影响企业在市场上的优势。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">我们分析一下在一个裸板上从头写一个裸片程序的过程。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">首先，我们要把</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 芯片和启动程序所必需的其他芯片进行寄存器设置层面的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">初始化，再写一些启动程序的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言代码，因为内存需要初始化，才能向其中加载</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内容。可以将要操作的寄存器地址直接定义为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言的宏，对寄存器的所有设置都</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">封装为对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言函数的调用，在很多嵌入式系统中都能看到类似的定义。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p017_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

---

## Page 18

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">对内存的初始化会比较麻烦，目前，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的线性地址和物理地址是有区别的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">线性地址是指</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的寻址空间，例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">32</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 位的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的线性地址空间的大小是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">4GB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">物理地址是指外设的真实访问地址，需要映射到线性地址才能被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 直接访问。物</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">理内存的空间大小并不一定要</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">4GB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，只要线性内存的空间大小是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">4GB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 就可以了。内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">存和其他外设的物理地址在程序启动时具体会被映射到什么样的线性地址，还需要</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">查看各个芯片的应用手册才能知道。很多芯片还有特殊的映射结构和启动逻辑，在启</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">动的早期必须要具体问题具体对待，这也是各种各样驱动程序存在的原因。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">然后，我们就可以将裸片程序逻辑加载到内存，让</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 跳转到程序入口点，开</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">始执行自己编写的逻辑程序。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言就必须为内存划分块（全局区、代码区等），我们可以让编译器</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">完成这个工作，但是通常需要手动布局。当涉及堆或者很大的内存时，就需要考虑</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内存分配算法和页的划分了。有了页的划分就会发现，自己实际申请的内存并不一</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">定会使用，会有缺页异常。如果直接使用一大块连续的内存，自己在内存中组织自</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">己的数据结构，那么</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言的堆的概念也可以不实现。很多时候嵌入式开发会强制</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要求在运行过程中不得使用堆内存，而在程序执行的一开始就分配大块内存供自己</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用。编译可以采用专门用于裸片编程的编译器，例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Keil</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 开发工具。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">最后，我们需要初始化外部的设备。外部的设备都是由寄存器控制的，寄存器</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">通常是功能复用的，它通过写入功能号来执行功能，并通过查看一些寄存器的位来</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">确定状态。如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">PCI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 这种总线硬件更复杂，还会有单独映射的配置空间，网卡有相对</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">通用的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">MII</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中间层等，针对一类硬件的访问需要封装，而分类类型可大可小，逐层</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">封装就形成了硬件抽象层。比如同样是鼠标，不同商家的寄存器排列不同，那么我</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">们就得针对每一种鼠标都实现一个驱动，让驱动的上层接口与硬件抽象层相符。于</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是驱动和硬件抽象层的概念就产生了。为了响应不同外设的事件，需要提供程序中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">断的实现，同时</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也会对程序中断和异常处理提出要求，这时中断子系统的概念</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">就浮出水面了。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">操作系统的设计源于需求，如果仅仅为了满足专用需求，那么即使是多任务，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">最后也很大概率是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VxWorks</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的纯内核态方式。只有当通用需求产生的时候，区分用</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">户态和内核态才有意义。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第1 章 操作系统总览 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p018_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

---

## Page 19

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000">1.3  主要操作系统与Linux的对比 </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">1.3.1  Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">Android </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统一般指常见的发行版，例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ubuntu</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">OpenSuse</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fedora</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等，另</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">外，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统还存在大量的、不常见的发行版，例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Kali</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等。每一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">嵌入式硬件都可以看作携带了一个专用的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发行版。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统主要包括</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核、系统服务和其对应的配置文件、系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统目录结构、常用库、程序包、命令工具和图形设施。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都有基础的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、常用命令、图形系统、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ashmem</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，但是采用了不同的实现，这</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">些共有的部分可以看作一个最小</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统，在此之上的系统服务和组件是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 桌</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">面系统与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统的主要区别。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1.  init </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核规定要有一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进程存在，通常</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进程承担系统服务管理的职责。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">继承自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">System V</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 风格的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统比较简单，目前仍被应用在嵌入式系统中。后来，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">大部分的发行版都采用了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">systemd</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 软件作为系统服务管理程序，而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 采用了自</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">己编写的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 工具，通过自定义的一套配置文件管理</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中系统服务的启动。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">大部分的系统服务都会有配置文件，配置文件被用来改变系统服务的行为，在桌面</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发行版下的大部分系统服务的配置文件都位于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">/etc/</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">目录下，而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的则位</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">/system/etc/</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">目录下，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 为了与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 目录结构兼容，将根目录的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">etc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 目录链</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">接到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">/system/etc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 目录，以此能方便地复用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下的一些工具。因此从目录结构上</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">看，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与其他发行版虽然区别很大，但是有很多相似的地方。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2.</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> libc </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">所有的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统都会有一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 库，即运行时的加载器。大部分的桌面</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">发行版的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 库都是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">glibc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在嵌入式系统中有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">uClibc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">newlib</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等小型化的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 库，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 单独开发了一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">libc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 库，叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Bionic</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">glibc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 太过复杂，并且固定了很多</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">操作系统的行为方式，例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">DNS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的解析缓存也在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">glibc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中实现。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统对自定</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p019_img01.png)



![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p019_img02.png)
