## Page 20

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">制的需求很强，所以进行了自研，运行加载器</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ld.so</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也是重新开发的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ELF</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的文件格式上做了扩充，并且对应地设计了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 专用的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">linker</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 程序。在应用层</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">方面，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 可以兼容</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 不能直接兼容</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3.  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">常用命令</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统包含系统管理的常用命令，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">POSIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中也规定了要包含的这些命令。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在桌面</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发行版中通常包含大量的命令和常用库，而在小型发行版中通常只包</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">含必需的命令和共享库，甚至只包含一个集成必需的命令</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Busybox</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">POSIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 约定的命令，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中也会发现类似的结构。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">大部分的桌面</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发行版都会基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">yum</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 或者</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">apt</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的方式进行包管理，一个包</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">就是一个工具，或者说一个软件。在桌面版</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的组件大部分都是通过包的形</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">式进行安装后使用的。这种类似的包管理软件有很多，很多发行版都在乐此不疲地</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">推出自己专用的包管理软件。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中，由于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计对于使用者来说</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是封闭的，甚至不允许使用者使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">root</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 权限，所以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 不允许动态地安装、卸</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">载系统组件，常用的包管理的方法在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中被去除了，取而代之的是纯粹的应</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用市场和对应的应用程序包的管理方式。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">4.  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">图形系统</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在图形系统上，大部分的桌面</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发行版都基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">X</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 窗口协议（或者</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Wayland</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">协议），而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 则基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SurfaceFlinger</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的组件。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的图形化没有网络传输的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">需求，但是有跨进程渲染的需求，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SurfaceFlinger</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 会完成桌面相关的混合渲染，而在</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">X</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 协议中，所有的渲染都集中传输渲染指令给</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">X</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 服务，由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">X</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 服务进行渲染。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SurfaceFlinger</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计允许应用本身在自己的窗口内调用渲染指令进行内部渲染，而</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SurfaceFlinger</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 只负责组装渲染后期的呈现效果，这种架构节省了大量的渲染指令传</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">输的开销。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">5.  Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ashmem </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核还添加了两个比较显著的改动：一个是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，另一个是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ashmem</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是为了高性能且安全的跨进程通信的需求而设计的，这是因为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统服务层的设计需要大量的性能敏感的跨进程系统调用，而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 设计了一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SystemServer</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 组件，大量的系统服务存在于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SystemServer</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进程中，对系统服务的需</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第1 章 操作系统总览 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 21

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">求需要跨进程地去</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SystemServer</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中寻求支援，但</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 已有的跨进程通信方案不能</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">满足</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的系统设计需求。高性能且安全的跨进程通信方式几乎是每个系统都</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要面对的问题。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Ashmem</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是匿名共享内存的实现，其实现方式比较简单，主要作用</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">也是跨进程地共享内存块和提供给</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 虚拟机使用。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">1.3.2  Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> 下</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> 运行环境的发展</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 程序不是一个最新的需求，从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1997</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 年开始，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SFU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SUA</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Project Astoria</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Islandwood</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Drawbridge</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等项目都持续在做这</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">件事情。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Interix</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 组件或者叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows Services for UNIX (SFU)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1999</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 年开始就提供</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 程序的能力，后来该组件在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows Vista</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 7</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">版本的时候升级为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SUA</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 8.1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 版本的时候正式被移除。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这类技术的特点是在编译和运行时使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">POSIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 库的程序的环境，且不提供</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 二进制文件的运行支持，也就是说，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SUA</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上运行的程序依然是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">exe</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 格式的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 10</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 版本的时候，有一个需求子项目叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Project Astoria</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，该项目能</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">够让</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 10</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 版本直接运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ARM</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 程序。但是在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2016</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 年，这个项目被叫停，只</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">留下了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">iOS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的兼容层</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Islandwood </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">项目。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Project Astoria</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 项目投入了很多人力，但它</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内部所产生的技术被一个崭新的项目</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 所使用，这个崭新的项目就是我们现在熟</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">知的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 子系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Islandwood</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">iOS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的应用需要重新编译，而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Project Astoria</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 项目是二进制层面</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的支持，这与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计思路一样。除了基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Project Astoria</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的一些工作，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 还</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">从其他项目借鉴了另外一个技术：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Drawbridge</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 项目的技术，也是一种新的虚拟化思路，它在用户</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">空间直接运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ELF</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 格式的文件，所用到的系统调用可以在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核里面直接模</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">拟。内核空间实现一个目标平台的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 支持，叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico Provider</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Drawbridge</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表了一种需求，就是把操作系统当作库来进行虚拟化运行。关于</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Drawbridge</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，有一篇论文是描述如何将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 7</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 作为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Library OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来运行的，其中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用到的技术就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">pico</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Graphene</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 实现了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统调用的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Library OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，但遗憾的是</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Graphene</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 只能运行在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统上。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p021_img01.png)



![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p021_img02.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 22

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">有一个项目叫</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">LKL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，其设计思路是将整个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核变成一个库。但是在使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">LKL</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的时候，需要直接用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">LKL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 链接应用程序，这使得原本依赖外部系统调用的程序就不</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">需要系统调用了。这其实是一个消灭系统调用的思路，而不是转换的思路。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">目前，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的兼容性只支持</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 8.1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 版本以上的系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">对应的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 技术也继承了同样的问题，并且目前还不支持</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">32</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 位系统，定制性也差，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">出了问题没办法修补。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Library OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计思路与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一致的，但是目前没有在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Library OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，只有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Graphene</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 能在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系列操作系统上运行</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Colinux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计思路也是类似的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表了微软一个具有战略性高度的项目，其直接从根本上改变了整个</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计方式，使得开源集成虚拟化变得更加彻底。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在本质上是一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">完整的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核，用户可以自己编译</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核以替换</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中使用的内核，这</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">体现出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在兼容性上做得很好。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">谷歌的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">gVisor</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表了另外一种思路，即在用户空间实现所有的系统调用，与</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的方式类似，通过截断系统调用，使得系统调用在用户空间完</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">成，这能保持内核代码的最小化。类似的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VBox</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也有同样的设计思路，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VBox</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 里</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">面有一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Recompiler</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 组件，可以动态地截断系统调用和中断以重新处理，但是性能</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">非常差。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">腾讯傲其实就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的概念，只是由自己实现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico Provider</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，并且自己</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">提供</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的接口。将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的系统调用在内核中重新实现一遍，这样的最大</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">好处是可以做到从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Window XP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows 10</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的全系统兼容，坏处是内核模块的系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统调用的完整实现工作量巨大，且</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">x64</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的方案需要创新。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">网易星云内核是全用户空间的内核模拟实现，其设计思路与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 类似，但是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">不依赖</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pico-process</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在用户空间实现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统调用和相关文件系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">1.3.3  Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> 的对比</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">微内核系统</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计大量地参考了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计，同时还可以看到</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">很多来自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计思想。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 使用了大量的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的思想，同为微内核设计的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 毫不避讳</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第1 章 操作系统总览 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 23

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">地继承了这个设计。内核管理的每一个资源都是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，打开每个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都有对应</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。在微内核中必须组织进程、线程之类的调度单元，这种操作系统一路</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">发展下来所沉淀的架构不可能被直接抛弃。安全性是附加在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">已经增加用户空间的调度接口，但是并不意味着微内核就不介入调度了，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的用户空间调度接口至今应用都很少。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 希望拥有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在图形方面（也可以说是硬件支持）的优势，又羡</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">慕</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核丰富的功能，而且其从一开始就知道自己不会长期依赖</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 更像一个操作系统架构层，验证的是操作系统的架构设计思想。在验证过程</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">中，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的内核早期只能采用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，没有更好的选择。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的下层替换，但是这个替换并不是代码层面上的，而是架构层面的。现在的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">AOSP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 源代码已经可以直接编译出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HarmonyOS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 操作系统的下层</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核也并不限于特定的内核，这种内核与系统解耦和的方式是操作系统发展的一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">新趋势。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下表示事件的设计是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Event</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下类似的设计是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Signal</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。这两个设</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">计完全不一样，但是又有很多相似的地方。谷歌经过深入的思考和实践，认为两者</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是可以结合的，尤其是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Plan 9</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Namespace</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 注入的通信方式和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Golang</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言设计中积</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">累的管道通信方法给两者结合提供了更多的思路。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中，状态、事件和</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">信号可以分别抽象为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Signal</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Event</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 三种互相结合的模型。每个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">32</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个信号集，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Event</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也是一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，且可以说是最简单的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的信</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">号集的变化代表</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 状态的变化，也就是说可以将信号与状态协调成一个概念。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">谷歌提取这些设计的核心本质，保留它们的各自优点，就形成了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Signal</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 模型。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在微内核层次完全抛弃了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的用户权限概念，改为了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 权限，甚至让整个虚拟化都建立在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对应的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的权限上。很</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的系统调用都要传入一个进程的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，这个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 决定了这</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">个系统调用有没有权限继续运作下去。虚拟化和沙箱技术是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的一个发展趋</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">势，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 从设计层面就直接做到了。所以说</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 更像是一个没有包袱</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统的重构，保留了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的大部分优点。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的进程间互写内存，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">process_vm_writev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统调用也能做</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">到类似的事情。进程间互相传递</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 一个很好用的资源传递的功</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">能。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下，想要将一个被打开的资源传递给另外一个进程，早期除了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fork</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 技</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">10</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p023_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 24

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">术，没有别的方法可以完成，后来出现了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SCM</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 技术，即通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UNIX Domain Socket</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">来直接传递</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">fd</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计中重度使用了这个功能。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 一个很大的设计问</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">题是太过依赖父子关系，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的问题是太不依赖父子关系，导致进程间缺乏有</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">效的组织。较新的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 版本已经很注重进程间关系的组织，或多或少地引入了</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的进程关系树模型。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计在相互融合的过程中都有一些对原生设计的违背，导</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">致整个操作系统看起来不太和谐，这个问题在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统中被放大了。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统重度依赖</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个试图让各个进程都可以很方便地通信、交换资源</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的设计，这个设计对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来说实现起来非常困难。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对于资源的进程隔离一直</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是一个很重要的发展方向，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 反其道而行之，要求进程之间大门敞开。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 既然是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 架构的落地承载，自然重度依赖</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。于是，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Golang</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中成</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">功实践的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Channel</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的思想在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中落地。传递</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，只需要把</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">放进</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Channel</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中，使得原进程自动失去该资源，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Channel</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对面的进程自动获得该资源。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内存块本身就是资源，也是可以有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 倾向于使用纯粹的内核</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">数据结构来组织整个线性地址空间，而并不用对象来表示。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 为了落实其自身</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的架构设计了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ashmem</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，用内存文件系统生硬地设计了带有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的内核块。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的底层内存管理是带有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的，叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Section</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Section</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">64KB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在往上层暴露的时候，仍然没有选择直接把</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Section</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 给用户用，而是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">进行了封装。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ashmem</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，但</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 没有提供内存文件系统这种概念，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">只能使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Section</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内存进行模拟。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 直接具有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Mem FS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 这种量身打造的文件</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在内核中使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Section</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和对应</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的方式，证明可以同时管理内存块和文</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">件映射，还可以向上提供更高层的内存分配机制。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 并没有直接采用</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Section</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 机制，而是创造性地设计了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Pager</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VMO</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">VMAR</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 这几种对象，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这几种对象将连续内存和页进行了面向对象的抽象，克服了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">granulary</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">固定的问题。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下对任务的组织采用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">job</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、进程、线程、纤程四个维度。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 同</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">样是在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的基础上进行增强的：进程组织成</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">job</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，进程下有线程。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下还有一个让人印象深刻的设计，就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Completion Port</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。当有大量的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">事件发生的时候，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Completion Port</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 将这些事件抽象为对一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">HANDLE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 发送的数据包</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">消息。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中，类似的事情使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">epoll</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ppoll</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等事件集合机制。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 作为一个</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第1 章 操作系统总览 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p024_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 25

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在服务端市场占有率第一的操作系统，其对并发问题的处理是非常好的（这里是指</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">技术层面，而不是架构层面）。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 一个显著的优势是把大部分用户空间的锁实现都抽象成对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">futex</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统调用</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的依赖。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">futex</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的实际意义其实跟锁没有任何关系，只是一个等待条件并且唤醒对应</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的线程的机制，也就是一个单纯的线程的同步机制。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 成功地做到让各种各样的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">锁都依赖一个简单的同步机制来实现目的，好的抽象设计正是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 要学习和</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">借鉴的。而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Mutex</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CriticalSection</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RWLOCK</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等系统锁，有的要跨</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">进程使用，有的只支持在进程内运行，它们全部都是黑盒，并且各自独立，这显然</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">不是好的系统锁该有的样子。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在调度算法上，操作系统产业界都逐渐向</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fair Scheduling</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（公平调度）过渡，尤</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">其是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 也同样使用了公平调度的思路。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">隔离性是目前</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都在面临的一个问题，服务端先对隔离性发起</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">重度需求。一时间，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 虚拟化技术如雨后春笋般蓬勃发展。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 近年来奋起直追，试图追赶并超越</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在虚拟化上的优势，同时伴</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">随自己的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">UWP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 技术对隔离性的强烈需求，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 创造了属于自己的隔离性，并</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">且试图侵蚀</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的阵地。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 技术的发展不遗余力，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 看到了虚拟化的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">威力。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的隔离性是一个“深入骨髓”的经典设计，深刻体现了整个架构</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的隔离性重构，既没有我们熟知的操作系统级别的文件系统，也没有根目录，以每</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">个进程为单位，只能看到自己的私有目录，其完整地去掉了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fork</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 还是允</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">许</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在进程间进行继承的，所以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fork</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 概念选择性支持。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 下的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">子进程要对父进程进行减法操作，一些变动会导致减法操作不到位，从而出现很多</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">安全问题。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fork</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计并不是为了隔离性而设计的，相反，它是完全共享数据，也</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是一个完全的反隔离设计。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Zircon</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 微内核是一个最能匹配当前所有场景应用的架构设计。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Zircon</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 提供了系统调用集，但是又把大量的工作交给了服务。服务也是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">落地得非常好的一个概念，是微内核必备的匹配组件。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的架构设计了大量的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">服务，例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SurfaceFlinger</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Zygo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的宏内核做了大量的服务，但是也不够</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">全面，还需要用户空间的服务来补全。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在架构层面，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个设计和实现都非常优秀的系统，但是其反应速度</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">太慢，在适应性上远不如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 系统设计的平衡性、隔离性和控制性都刚</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">刚好，它可以由一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">OEM</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进行强控制，也可以完全不被控制，是一个很灵活的社</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">12</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p025_img01.png)
