## Page 26

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">会化设计。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在驱动层面，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Zircon</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 开放了用户程序中断处理的系统调用，相当于内核层面直</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">接对驱动进行了应用层的委派，但又不是委派给应用程序的，而是委派给</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">DDK</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">即一个专门的允许闭源驱动存在的框架。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Zircon</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 架构的主要学习对象；</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个很好的验证算法逻辑的对象；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 则是一次尝试，一次架构设计的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">验证和社会性的学习积累，也是一个独立于内核的操作系统产品。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">整个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的核心</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IPC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 调用接口是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">FIDL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia Interface Definition </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Language</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 接口定义语言），这种描述性的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IPC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 表达方式简直与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Binder</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">如出一辙。随着</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Flutter</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的逐步推广，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 模型的有效性正在由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 一步一步地验证。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Volume Manager</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上实现得非常好，但是在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上的实现非常不成</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">功。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Mount</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（挂载）是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上的一个基本功能，这个设计非常优秀。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">网络文件系统在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中实现得都不算好，但是又各有千秋，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">WSL</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">中对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">9P</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 协议的应用被谷歌注意到了，但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">9P</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 又迟迟没有落地，变成了“纸上谈兵”。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 使用了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都有的描述性接口，并对建立连接的概念进</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">行了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 设计。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">9P</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在不断的实践过程中暴露了比</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 本身的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 还多的性能</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">问题。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">显示问题是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 桌面系统的最大问题，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">DirectX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 到驱动的软件结构</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">得到显卡厂商的大力支持。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 积累了大量的渲染经验，这让</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 充分意识到渲染部分的重要性。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Android</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SurfaceFlinger</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计和游戏</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">本体渲染的隔离，让传统的单线程渲染显得非常笨重。渲染子系统本身要负责对任</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">务的调度和内存的管理，这是现代渲染架构已经认清的问题。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 作为一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">新时代的操作系统自觉地对渲染做出让步，让渲染子系统能够承担越来越多的自主</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">性工作。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Direct Compute</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等显卡计算技术已经在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 调度层面认识到计算方面的不</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">足，可以预见的是，在未来，计算技术也会更多地交给渲染管线来执行。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 像两个兄弟，当</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 满足不了社会对操作系统的需求时，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">就由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来满足；在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 顶不住压力的地方，就由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来代替。双方在迭</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">代的过程中终于逐渐对领域层进行了划分。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在满足需求的过程中，选择了优先</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">满足服务端和可裁剪的嵌入式需求；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在满足需求的过程中，选择了优先满</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">足桌面。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个新时代的操作系统，它的诞生几乎是建立在充分了解</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第1 章 操作系统总览 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">13</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的弊端和优势基础之上的。变化的是需求，让架构更好地适应快</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">速变化的需求是一个操作系统长期发展的重要保证。现在，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 仍然</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在坚持不断地创新和突破，以满足社会的需求。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Fuchsia OS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是站在巨人肩膀上的设</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">计，因为脱离时代的跳跃式发展是不存在的，技术的演进必须要在已有的技术基础</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">之上进行哲学层面、设计层面和实现层面的创新。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">14</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 28

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:25.98pt;color:#000000">第2 章 </span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialBlack';font-size:42.00pt;color:#ffffff">2 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZDBSJW--GB1-0';font-size:25.98pt;color:#000000">系统结构 </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000">2.1  Linux内核整体结构 </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核的结构中使用了很多“约定俗成”的约定，这些约定大部分被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">语言开发者所熟知，并被广泛应用到日常使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言的开发中。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核在层次定义中一般使用面向对象的结构体抽象方式，这种方式首先定</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">义一个结构体（包含各种函数指针并且管理其列表），下层通过生成这样一个被定义</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的结构体，来将操作函数赋值给该结构体的对应域；然后调用上层的注册函数，将</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">信息注册到上层，这样上层就可以用统一的函数调用不同的下层接口。这种方式使</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言，同时融入了面向对象的编程思路。一个典型的例子如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct address_space_operations { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*writepage)(struct page *page, structwriteback_control *wbc); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*readpage)(struct file *, struct page *); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*writepages)(structaddress_space *, structwriteback_control *); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*set_page_dirty)(struct page *page); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*readpages)(struct file *filp, structaddress_space *mapping, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">structlist_head *pages, unsigned nr_pages); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*write_begin)(struct file *, structaddress_space *mapping, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">loff_tpos, unsigned len, unsigned flags, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct page **pagep, void **fsdata); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*write_end)(struct file *, structaddress_space *mapping, </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p028_img01.png)

## Page 29

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">loff_tpos, unsigned len, unsigned copied, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct page *page, void *fsdata); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">sector_t (*bmap)(structaddress_space *, sector_t); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">void (*invalidatepage) (structpage *, unsigned int, unsigned int); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*releasepage) (struct page *, gfp_t); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">void (*freepage)(struct page *); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">ssize_t (*direct_IO)(structkiocb *, structiov_iter *iter, loff_t </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">offset); </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*migratepage) (structaddress_space *,struct page *, struct page </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*, enummigrate_mode); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*launder_page) (struct page *); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*is_partially_uptodate) (struct page *, unsigned long, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned long); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">void (*is_dirty_writeback) (struct page *, bool *, bool *); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*error_remove_page)(structaddress_space *, struct page *); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">int (*swap_activate)(structswap_info_struct *sis, struct file *file, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">sector_t *span); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">void (*swap_deactivate)(struct file *file); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当上层调用一个下层的函数时，一般有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 种返回值的方式：第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 种，通过语言</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">规定的函数返回值；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 种，通过传递指向结果指针的方式；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 种，使用回调函数，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">回调函数通常是由调用者提供的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核系统按照功能分类可以分成几个大型的子系统，其通过上下层通信的方式</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">将内核各个子系统有效地区分了层级关系，使得系统架构更清晰。虽然这个方法并</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">不一定是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 首创的，但大量的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 语言程序都受到这种风格的影响。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核中的系统大体分为纵向系统、横向系统和独立子系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）纵向系统是指具体的功能模块，这些模块总体像一片森林，不同的功能树</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">下面有很多的层次。例如一个用户端对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">USB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 文件的操作，要走完内核中的很多个层</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">次（有文件系统层、缓存层、通用块层、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">SCSI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 层、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">USB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 层），每个层次的内部又分</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">为多个子层次。但</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核尽量将一个层次内部的子层次数量控制在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个以内：</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">为上层提供统一接口的接口层，实现主要逻辑的功能中间层，以及统一为下层不同</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">驱动提供编程接口的驱动层。不同层次有不同的分工，按照顺序完成工作，一整条</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">链路下来就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的一个纵向的子系统。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）横向系统是被各个子系统所使用的、以统一的方式对外提供服务的组件。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">16</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p029_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 30

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">横向系统主要有固定点钩子和文件系统两种：固定点钩子如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">audit</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">trace</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">netfilter</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">等；文件系统如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">group</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">proc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sys</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 等。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）独立子系统是内核中功能相对独立的模块。比较大型的独立子系统主要包</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">括调度、锁、信号、中断、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">DMA</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、时钟、内存管理、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sysrq</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、驱动子系统、安全子系</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">统、进程间通信等；还包括一些常用的比较小型的组件，主要包括</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">workqueue</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">tasklet</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">打印等。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.1.1  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">内核模块</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核模块是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 支持动态功能扩展的最主要机制。在内核代码中有很多模块，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用户也可以编写外部的模块，再将模块动态添加到内核中执行即可。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核的主</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">要代码是遵守</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">General Public License</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）协议的，其内部暴露给模块使用。如果</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用户在内核模块进行编程时要调用内核内部的定义，就需要将自己完整的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 公开，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的传染机制。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">有很多公司可以不必遵守</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 协议。例如，做</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NTFS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 文件系统内核模块驱动的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Tuxera</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 公司，其最著名的产品是用户端开源的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NTFS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 文件系统驱动</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ntfs-3g</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，然而这</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">个驱动的工作效率并不高，另外该公司还提供闭源的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NTFS</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核模块驱动，如果要</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">使用该闭源驱动则需要购买。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">模块的执行原理与其他功能组件类似，都是由内核约定好要调用的函数，再由</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">模块开发者填充实现这些函数，在添加、关闭模块的时候内核模块调度系统就会执</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">行用户注册的自己实现的函数。在模块开发中比较典型的是初始化函数和退出函数，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">模块代码示例如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static int __initinit(void) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">    printk(&quot;Hi module!\n&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">    return 0; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static void __exit exit(void) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">    printk(&quot;Bye module!\n&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">17</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p030_img01.png)



![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p030_img02.png)

## Page 31

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">module_init(init); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">module_exit(exit); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MODULE_DESCRIPTION(&quot;Hello World !!&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MODULE_AUTHOR(&quot;liujingyang&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MODULE_LICENSE(&quot;GPL&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">可以看出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">module_init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">module_exit</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 就是注册约定函数的调用。模块内部定义</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的钩子函数是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">static</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，目的是只内部可见。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">__init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">__exit</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GCC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的特性，回收明确</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">表示无用的代码。标记为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">__init</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的函数会被放入</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">.init.text</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代码段，这个代码段不会再</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">被用到，在模块加载完后会被回收，以节省内存。上面代码的最后三行是三个宏，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">如果缺少</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">MODULE_LICENSE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏的版权声明，那么在加载的时候内核就会告警</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Warning: loading hello.ko will taint the kernel: no license</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">”。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在编程的时候可以指定模块要接受的参数，这个参数也可以在用户空间使用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在模块加载之后，用户空间通过“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">echo-n ${value} &gt; /sys/module/${modulename}/ </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">parameters/ ${parm}</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">”就可以修改模块参数。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">原则上内核模块在被使用的过程中不可以被卸载，但可以被强制卸载，或者找</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">到所有使用它的单位按照顺序将其关闭或卸载，使模块的被引用计数变为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">0</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。而在</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">加载的时候必须保证模块与运行中的内核相容。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">insmod</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">rmmod</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是用户端加载和卸</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">载模块的常用命令。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">由于模块可以由外部代码编写，内核的版本又有很多个，所以内核必须确保该</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">模块是使用当前内核代码编译出来的，否则在执行时会出现错误。每个模块在编译</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">时都会从内核目录中获得版本号，运行中的内核在插入新的模块时会检测签名是否</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一致，若不一致就不会加载。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">模块签名有两层含义：一层是版本号；另一层是哈希签名。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xor</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核模块的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">modinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 输出如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2-1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 所示。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2-1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中显示没有对模块进行签名，如果对模块签名了，则会在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">modinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">多出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">signer</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sig_key</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sig_hashalgo 3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个域。如果在编译内核的时候选择了</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">图</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">2-1  xor</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 内核模块的</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">modinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 输出</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 32

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CONFIG_MODULE_SIG_FORCE</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏，那么有的内核就会拒绝加载没有签名的模块。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xor</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核模块是在压缩过程中会用到的一个内核模块，这个内核模块包含一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">core_initcall</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的初始化顺序指定特性，对外只导出了一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xor_blocks</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 函数。下面列举</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一个完整的内核模块，具体代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#include &lt;linux/module.h&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#include &lt;linux/gfp.h&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#include &lt;linux/raid/xor.h&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#include &lt;linux/jiffies.h&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#include &lt;linux/preempt.h&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#include &lt;asm/xor.h&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#ifndef XOR_SELECT_TEMPLATE </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define XOR_SELECT_TEMPLATE(x) (x) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#endif </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">/* The xor routines to use.  */ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static struct xor_block_template *active_template; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">void </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">xor_blocks(unsigned int src_count, unsigned int bytes, void *dest, void </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">**srcs) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned long *p1, *p2, *p3, *p4; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">p1 = (unsigned long *) srcs[0]; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (src_count == 1) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">active_template-&gt;do_2(bytes, dest, p1); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">p2 = (unsigned long *) srcs[1]; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (src_count == 2) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">active_template-&gt;do_3(bytes, dest, p1, p2); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

## Page 33

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">p3 = (unsigned long *) srcs[2]; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (src_count == 3) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">active_template-&gt;do_4(bytes, dest, p1, p2, p3); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">p4 = (unsigned long *) srcs[3]; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static __exit void xor_exit(void) { } </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MODULE_LICENSE(&quot;GPL&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">/* when built-in xor.o must initialize before drivers/md/md.o */ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">core_initcall(calibrate_xor_blocks); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">module_exit(xor_exit); </span>
<span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">以上整个模块被声明为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，唯一的导出函数是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xor_blocks()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，其属性也是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">结尾的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">core_initcall()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是模块的初始化函数，当模块加载的时候，需要先运行这个函</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">数。当模块被内联编译进内核的时候，还需要指定模块被初始化的顺序，这个顺序</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">就是由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">core_initcall()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">系列函数组成的，具体代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define pure_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 0) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define core_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 1) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define core_initcall_sync(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 1s) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define postcore_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 2) </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">22</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p035_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

---

## Page 36

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define postcore_initcall_sync(fn) __define_initcall(fn, 2s) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define arch_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 3) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define arch_initcall_sync(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 3s) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define subsys_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 4) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define subsys_initcall_sync(fn) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 4s) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define fs_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 5) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define fs_initcall_sync(fn) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 5s) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define rootfs_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, rootfs) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define device_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 6) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define device_initcall_sync(fn) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 6s) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define late_initcall(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 7) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define late_initcall_sync(fn)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__define_initcall(fn, 7s)</span><span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当模块之间存在依赖关系，为了一个模块必须在另外模块之前完成初始化，就</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">需要使用带初始化顺序的初始化方法。这个初始化顺序也是</span><span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核在启动时的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内部初始化的顺序。</span><span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">整个</span><span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xor</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 模块的原理就是先通过初始化函数选择一个计算函数，再通过暴露出</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">来的</span><span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xor_blocks()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数直接调用在初始化时选择的计算函数进行计算。</span><span style="font-family:'Cambria';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.1.2  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">内核符号表</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核符号表是内核内部各个功能模块之间互相调用的纽带，各个模块之间依赖</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数调用进行通信。加载的模块所导出的函数通过导出操作就可以被其他模块定位并</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">调用，代码示例如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static struct request *blk_old_get_request(structrequest_queue *q, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">intrw,gfp_tgfp_mask) </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct request *rq; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">BUG_ON(rw != READ &amp;&amp;rw != WRITE); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">create_io_context(gfp_mask, q-&gt;node); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">blk_get_request</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 使用了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">EXPORT_SYMBOL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，所以可以被任何其他的模块和内核使</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用（仍然需要遵守</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 协议），而使用了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">part_round_stats</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数则声明自己只能被遵守</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 协议的模块使用。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 相比</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">EXPORT_SYMBOL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的区别在于每个模块都可以声明自己遵守的协议。比如遵守</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">协议的模块，可以在自己的模块代码中添加：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">MODULE_LICENSE(&quot;GPL&quot;)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，之后就</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">能用另外一个模块调用被本模块封装之后的函数。只有设置了遵守</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 协议的模块</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">才可以被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 定义导出的系统调用。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cat /proc/kallsyms</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 命令能打印出包含加载模块的内核当前的符号表，可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">more /boot/System.map</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 命令查看内核二进制符号列表，也可以通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">nm vmlinux</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">查看内核符号列表，但只能显示内核中的所有符号，模块中的符号要另行查看。通</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">nm module_name</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 可以查看模块的符号列表，但是得到的是相对地址，只有加载</span>

## Page 38

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">后才会分配绝对地址。内核当前符号表如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2-2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 所示。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000">2.2  Linux内核数据结构 </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核数据结构与用户端的数据结构并没有理论上的不同，但是内核数据结构通</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">常比用户端的数据结构更加注重性能和内核业务场景。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.2.1  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">链表与哈希表</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">链表既有弹性，又能在弹性伸缩的过程中保持已有的内容不变。链表可以把在</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">离散时间到达的数据结构串起来，使其更容易被索引，并且不需要移动之前的内容，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">但缺陷是数据在内存中是离散的，不利于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU cache</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 加速和批量管理。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核哈希表是由链表群组成的，每一个哈希桶（即每一个哈希的值位置）都是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一个链表。哈希表有很多种实现方法，不同实现方法的主要区别就在于处理哈希冲</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">突的方式。在内核中采用的是开链的哈希表，主要使用双向链表，而这个链表在做</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">开链哈希桶时要有针对性地优化：使头部节点只占一个指针的大小。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">总体来说，哈希表是一个大数组，数组的索引就是哈希的结果，但是这样可能</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">会出现多个值对应同一个索引值的问题，所以所有的哈希表都需要解决哈希（值）</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">冲突的问题。针对解决哈希冲突的方法可以将哈希表分为三种：开链哈希表、多级</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">哈希表和布谷鸟（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Cuckoo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）哈希表，下面对这三种哈希表进行详细介绍。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）开链哈希表，使用链表来解决冲突，这是在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核中采用的方法，也</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是在实际使用中最常见的方法。由于哈希表具有稀疏的特征，所以并不是所有的哈</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 39

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">希桶（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）都存在内容，但不存在内容时根本不需要哈希表的存在。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的值</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">可以直接设置为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NULL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，这就要求所使用的链表的头部尽可能只占一个指针的位置，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的概念，是一个头部只占一个指针大小的特殊双向哈希表。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）多级哈希表，一般用在性能非常敏感的场所，例如，华为方舟编译器的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">vtable</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的实现就采用了二级哈希表，一级哈希表是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">32</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">slot</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的数组，若对索引到同一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的不同值进行一次再哈希，则在数组前面的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">31</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">slot</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中使用二次哈希的值作</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">为索引来存放内容。如果发现经过二次哈希的结果仍然发生冲突，就在最后一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">slot</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的位置进行特殊标记，然后重新生成一个二级哈希，在二级哈希中解决冲突，但二</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">级哈希会发生冲突的概率很小，所以二级哈希一般使用链表即可。这样做的好处是，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在大部分情况下，一级哈希不需要遍历链表，而是一个直接的索引，性能非常好。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）布谷鸟哈希表，这种哈希表曾经在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">DPDK</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中被广泛应用，它的原理是每个</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都是一个数组，索引的结果在数组中进行再哈希，只是当二级哈希出现冲突</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的时候，布谷鸟哈希表不进行额外的内存申请，而是到其他的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中寻找是否存</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在可用的空的位置。布谷鸟哈希表的特点是需要的内存大小是固定的，在使用文件</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">作为哈希表的存储介质时，可以直接映射文件到内存以加载哈希表。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在这三种哈希表中，性能最好的且可以最大程度实现无锁的是多级哈希表，跨</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">进程共享首选布谷鸟哈希表，最节省内存的是开链哈希表。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.2.2  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">双向链表</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">双向链表很容易做成一个环，即将起始的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">prev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 域设为最后一个数据，将最后一</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">个数据的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 设为起始数据。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">include/linux/list.h</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中实现的双向链表的节点不包含</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">实际的数据域，而在具体的数据结构中包含链表的节点。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">理论上链表功能是数据结构功能的一部分。当一段代码拿到一个数据结构的实</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">例后，就可以通过访问其中的链表域来确定其链表情况。在使用链表定位到某一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">实例后，就可以使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">container_of</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏定位到这个结构体本身。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">container_of</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏的作用</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是在已知结构体某个域的指针的情况下，求出结构体实例的指针，其原理是根据结构</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">体定义得出已知指针的偏移，用已知指针减去这个偏移就是结构体的指针，代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define container_of(ptr, type, member) ({ \ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">     const typeof( ((type *)0)-&gt;member ) *__mptr = (ptr); \ </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">26</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p039_img01.png)



![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p039_img02.png)
