## Page 40

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">     (type *)( (char *)__mptr - offsetof(type,member) );})  </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">container_of</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏并不只用于链表节点到真实数据结构体的映射，也可以在其他域</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">使用。双向链表的节点定义如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct list_head { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">        struct list_head *next, *prev; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> }; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这个双向链表的核心是一个头部，其与用户端链表的显著不同是没有数据域。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在时钟源管理中（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">kernel/time/clocksource.c</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">），也是通过链表对所有的可用时钟</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">进行管理的。一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是两个指针的大小，对链表的初始化定义如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define LIST_HEAD_INIT(name) { &amp;(name), &amp;(name) } </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define LIST_HEAD(name) \ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct list_head name = LIST_HEAD_INIT(name) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static LIST_HEAD(clocksource_list); </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">相当于定义了：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct list_head clocksource_list = {&amp;clocksource_list, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">&amp;clocksource_list}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">也就是定义并初始化了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">clocksource_list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 这个双向链表。添加一个时钟源到链表，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static void clocksource_enqueue(struct clocksource *cs) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct list_head *entry = &amp;clocksource_list; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct clocksource *tmp; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">list_for_each_entry(tmp, &amp;clocksource_list, list) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (tmp-&gt;rating &lt; cs-&gt;rating) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">break; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">entry = &amp;tmp-&gt;list; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">list_add(&amp;cs-&gt;list, entry); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">首先，遍历这个链表，由于链表本身只是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct list_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 类型，其中的节点也是</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct list_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 类型，因此在遍历的时候使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list_for_each_entry</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，通过第一个参数传</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">27</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p040_img01.png)

## Page 41

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">入</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct clocksource * </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，就可以让每个遍历得到的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">entry</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的类型都转换为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">clocksource * </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在遍历的逻辑中就可以直接使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct clocksource *</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">类型的变量来进</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">行处理。然后，通过对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">tmp-&gt;rating</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cs-&gt;rating</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进行大小对比，找到第一个比</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cs-&gt;rating</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">小的时钟源，跳出遍历循环，在第一个比</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cs-&gt;rating</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的值小的位置进行插入，从而就</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">实现了一个以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">rating</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的大小为维度的排序链表。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">也就是说，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">clocksource_list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct clocksource *</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">类型的双向排序链表，却</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">只使用了一个简单的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct list_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 为基本单位组织的双向链表结构。以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 为基本单位的双向链表结构就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核提供给其他组件的基础双向链</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">表数据结构，以下代码是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 遍历的定义。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define list_entry(ptr, type, member) \ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">container_of(ptr, type, member) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">#define list_for_each_entry(pos, head, member)  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">for (pos = list_entry((head)-&gt;next, typeof(*pos), member);  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">     &amp;pos-&gt;member != (head);  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">     pos = list_entry(pos-&gt;member.next, typeof(*pos), member)) </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list_for_each_entry</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的实现过程就是，遍历通用类型的链表，对每一个元素都使</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">container_of</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏进行类型转换。整个过程的核心是向</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">container_of</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏传入链表在外</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">部结构体中的偏移，也就是第三个参数</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">member</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在第一个参数</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ptr</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的偏移。对于</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">clocksource_list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，使用了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list_for_each_entry(tmp, &amp;clocksource_list, list)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，也就是传入</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 这个域在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct clocksource</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的偏移，所以在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct clocksource</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中必然存在一</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">个叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的域，定义方式是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct list_head list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，否则就无法从链表得到外部的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">clocksource</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 指针。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.02pt;color:#000000">2.3  hlist </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">双向链表的缺点是如果有很多特别短的链表（比如只有一个节点或者空链表），</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">双向链表的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">prev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的头部就非常占用空间。哈希表使用哈希函数计算得到一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">地址，然后直接访问该地址的机制实现快速访问，但是哈希算法不可避免地会有哈</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">希冲突（多个输入产生了同一个地址输出），此时解决哈希冲突的方法就是使用哈希</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">桶，开链哈希表是哈希桶的常见实现方式，原理是在同一个计算地址的位置实现一</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">28</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p041_img01.png)

## Page 42

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">个链表，该链表链出所有哈希结果为本地址的值。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在通常情况下，哈希表大部分的域都是空白的，哈希表所需要的空间大小要提</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">前分配。一个双向链表的头部有两个指针的大小，这两个指针全部放入哈希表所分</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">配的空间，会比单链表的头部所占用的内存空间多一倍。所以内核专门设计了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">即只有一个指针大小的头部的双向链表。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的结构如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2-3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 所示。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">哈希链表在组织方式上的第一个节点与普通双向链表的不一样。节点定义如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">//</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">哈希桶的头节点</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_head {   </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">    struct hlist_node *first;//</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">指向每一个哈希桶的第一个节点的指针</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">};   </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">//</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">哈希桶的普通节点</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_node {   </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">    struct hlist_node *next;//</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">指向下一个节点的指针</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">    struct hlist_node **pprev;//</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">指向上一个节点的</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 指针的地址</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">};   </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 双向链表是环形的，而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 有特定的头部结构，其头部（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）只</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">有一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">first</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 域，用来指向第一个节点（一个头部只有一个整数大小）。首先</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_head</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">first</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 域指向一个双向链表，相当于在原来的双向链表上提取了一个钩子指针指向</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">开头的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 位置，然后将第一个节点的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">pprev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 指向</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，牺牲了从第一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">节点直接访问最后一个节点的能力，最后一个节点的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NULL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，相当于去掉了</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">双向链表从最后一个节点访问第一个节点的能力。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的开头位置添加一个节点，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static inline void hlist_add_head(struct hlist_node *n, struct hlist_head </span>

## Page 43

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*h) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_node *first = h-&gt;first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">n-&gt;next = first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (first) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">first-&gt;pprev = &amp;n-&gt;next; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">WRITE_ONCE(h-&gt;first, n); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">n-&gt;pprev = &amp;h-&gt;first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这么做其实是为了适应头部设计而引入的带“副作用”的解决方法。之所以要</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">设计头部为一个指针大小是因为提高哈希桶的空间利用率，而这个头部的引入导致</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">了第一个节点与后面节点的不同，因此，在理论上，所有相关的操作（添加、删除、</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">遍历等）都得特别照顾第一个节点（多一个特殊情况判断）。如果能从数据结构设计</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">上将这种特殊情况去掉无疑是最好的，而</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的设计做到了这一点。其</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">pprev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（对</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">应于双向链表的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">prev</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）并不是指向上一个节点的数据结构，而是指向上一个节点的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 域。这对于头部节点来说，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 结构体的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">first</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 域既是指向下一个节</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">点的指针，也是下一个节点指向上一个节点的指针，如此就能让所有节点对所有操</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">作都展现出几乎一样的接口了。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的最后一个节点的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的值是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NULL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，这个位置是固定的，而且是被浪费</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">掉的。这个节点的指针大小为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 字节（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">64</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 位），任何一个节点的指针值的最后一位</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">都必然是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">0</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 利用了对齐特性实现了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的变种</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 与普通</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的区别就在于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NULL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的表示方式是最后一位，但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 带来了更多有趣</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的使用方式。例如当需要暂时截断这个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的时候，可以不用将链表从</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中摘下来，而只是简单地在要截断的位置将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的最后一位设置为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 即</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">可，具体代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_nulls_head { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_nulls_node *first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_nulls_node { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_nulls_node *next, **pprev; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">从数据结构上看，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 有一样的数据结构，在内存布局上也是一</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">30</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p043_img01.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 44

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">样的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的网络管理子系统使用哈希表来管理所有的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 连接，所使用的链表就</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，我们以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">net/ipv4/tcp_ipv4.c</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ipv4</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 连接管理为例，来说明</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在哈希表中的应用。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">net/ipv4/tcp_ipv4.c</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 文件的开头有定义</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">tcp_hashinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 结构体，具体代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_ehash_bucket </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*ehash; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">spinlock_t  </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*ehash_locks; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned int </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">ehash_mask; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned int </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct kmem_cache </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*bind_bucket_cachep; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_bind_hashbucket *bhash; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned int </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">bhash_size; </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned int </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">lhash2_mask; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_listen_hashbucket *lhash2; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_listen_hashbucket  listening_hash[INET_LHTABLE_SIZE] </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">___cacheline_aligned_in_smp; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在以上</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo tcp_hashinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 结构体中定义了三个哈希表：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">已经建立的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 连接对应的哈希表，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bhash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bind</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 状态的哈希表，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">lhash2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">listening_hash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">listen</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 状态的哈希表。下面我们以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 为例进行说明。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的哈</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">希表被单独定义成一个文件，位于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">net/ipv4/inet_hashtables.c</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，里面包含了大部分</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">inet_hashinfo </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">结构体的定义和操作函数的实现。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 结构</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">体的时候，除了定义该结构体的全局变量，还需要对该结构体进行初始化。初始化</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">代码位于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">net/ipv4.c:tcp_init()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的初始化代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">tcp_hashinfo.ehash = </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">alloc_large_system_hash(&quot;TCP established&quot;, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">sizeof(struct inet_ehash_bucket), </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">thash_entries, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">17, /* one slot per 128 KB of memory */ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">0, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">&amp;tcp_hashinfo.ehash_mask, </span>

## Page 45

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">0, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">thash_entries ? 0 : 512 * 1024); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">for (i = 0; i &lt;= tcp_hashinfo.ehash_mask; i++) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">INIT_HLIST_NULLS_HEAD(&amp;tcp_hashinfo.ehash[i].chain, i); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (inet_ehash_locks_alloc(&amp;tcp_hashinfo)) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">panic(&quot;TCP: failed to alloc ehash_locks&quot;); </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">由上述可见，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 结构体的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 指针只简单地申请了一大块内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">存作为哈希表空间，每一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket entry</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的大小都是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sizeof(struct inet_ehash_bucket)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">具体代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_ehash_bucket { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_nulls_head chain; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一个简单的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 头部的封装，其大小是一个指针的大小，一共有</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">thash_entries</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个，这里的个数是这个哈希表中一共可以存储的元素个数。哈希表可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">根据元素总数和发生冲突的概率来计算得到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数，就是分配的内存数。这种计</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">算方式在理论上要不同情况不同对待，但是在内核中统一使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">log2(numentries)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">来进</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">行计算。对哈希表所需内存的估算可直接在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">alloc_large_system_hash()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这个内存分配</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数中完成，该函数位于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">mm/page_alloc.c</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，是直接对外提供内存分配服务的接口</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">alloc_large_system_hash()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 函数在分配内存的时候，只有当第三个参数</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">thash_entries</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">0</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的时候，才会使用第四个参数（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 初始化代码中的“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">17, </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">”）</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">来确定</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的个数。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">thash_entries</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是一个内核启动参数，可以在启动内核的时候</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">手动指定。对于未指定</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">entry</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数目情况下的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的计算，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">alloc_large_system_hash()</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数会根据</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">scale</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 得到的结果有一个通用的算法。最后得到的哈希表内存大小的计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">方式是：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucketsize &lt;&lt; 17</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，就是输入的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">scale</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的大小一共是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">128KB</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，这就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数组的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数量，再乘以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sizeof(struct inet_ehash_bucket)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内存的大小。每个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 在使用的时候都会对应一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的哈希链表，当该</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 没有被用到的时候，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上的值就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NULL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，也相当于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">head-&gt;first</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的值是</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">NULL</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，即空链表。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这个内存申请函数还传入了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">tcp_hashinfo.ehash_mask</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 函数，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">alloc_large_ </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">32</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p045_img01.png)

## Page 46

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">system_hash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 返回的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数量一定是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的整数倍，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1&lt;&lt;17-1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 就相当于这个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">数量的最大值，这个最大值在计算哈希索引的时候特别有用，代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static inline struct inet_ehash_bucket *inet_ehash_bucket( </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo *hashinfo, </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">unsigned int hash) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return &amp;hashinfo-&gt;ehash[hash &amp; hashinfo-&gt;ehash_mask]; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当从一个哈希值选择</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的索引的时候，直接使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hash &amp; hashinfo-&gt; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash_mask</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 就可以得到一个小于最大</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数的索引值，从而将哈希结果规约在数</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">组的索引范围内，定位到具体的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。向</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ehash</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的哈希表中添加一个元素，代码</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">bool inet_ehash_insert(struct sock *sk, struct sock *osk) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_hashinfo *hashinfo = sk-&gt;sk_prot-&gt;h.hashinfo; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct hlist_nulls_head *list; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct inet_ehash_bucket *head; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">spinlock_t *lock; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">bool ret = true; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">WARN_ON_ONCE(!sk_unhashed(sk)); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">sk-&gt;sk_hash = sk_ehashfn(sk); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">head = inet_ehash_bucket(hashinfo, sk-&gt;sk_hash); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">list = &amp;head-&gt;chain; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">lock = inet_ehash_lockp(hashinfo, sk-&gt;sk_hash); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">spin_lock(lock); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (osk) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">WARN_ON_ONCE(sk-&gt;sk_hash != osk-&gt;sk_hash); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">ret = sk_nulls_del_node_init_rcu(osk); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (ret) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">__sk_nulls_add_node_rcu(sk, list); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">spin_unlock(lock); </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

## Page 47

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return ret; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">上述代码中的参数</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">osk</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 代表要删除的条目。首先使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sk-&gt;sk_hash = sk_ehashfn(sk)</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">计算出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sk</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的哈希值，然后由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">head = inet_ehash_bucket(hashinfo, sk-&gt;sk_hash)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">得到该</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">哈希值对应的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，再对这个链表上锁，最后调用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的添加函数将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">sk</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的链</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">表添加到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">bucket</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的链表中。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">这里添加函数调用的是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">__sk_nulls_add_node_rcu</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，而不是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls_add_head</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">因为在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">include/linux/rculist_nulls.h</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 这个头文件中，对普通的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 进行了方法扩</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">充，使用的还是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">hlist_nulls</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的数据结构，只是增加了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RCU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 相关的方法。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RCU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是指内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">核的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RCU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 锁，只有在修改链表的时候需要加锁，在遍历访问链表时不需要加锁。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">哈希表的多级哈希就是为了可以高性能所以不加锁或者加小锁。在用户模式实</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">现的开链哈希表，无论是遍历还是修改都需要对整个链表进行加锁，这也是开链的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">方式在高性能哈希表中不被经常使用的原因。但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核提出了使用小锁的方</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">案，该方案可以极大地增强并行能力。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.3.1  llist </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的全称是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Lock-less NULL terminated single linked list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，意思是不需要加锁的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。在“生产者-消费者”模型下，如果有多个生产者和多个消费者，则生产者意</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">味着链表添加操作，消费者意味着链表删除操作。如果有多个生产者或者多个消费</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">者一起操作，就需要加锁，但加锁是高耗费的操作，为这个需求诞生的就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核实现的无锁</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 并不是在所有的情况下都无锁，可以使用的组合如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Wingdings2';font-size:10.50pt;color:#656565"></span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当多个生产者和多个消费者参与的时候，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_add</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_del_all</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">可以无须加锁并发使用。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Wingdings2';font-size:10.50pt;color:#656565"></span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当多个生产者和一个消费者参与的时候，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_add</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_del_first</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">可以无须加锁并发使用。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Wingdings2';font-size:10.50pt;color:#656565"></span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">遍历只可以发生在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_del_all</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 之后，也就是遍历不是无锁的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">从上述使用场景可以看出，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的使用场景是多个生产者对应一个或多个消费</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">者的情况。并且由于遍历不是无锁的，所以在设计上遍历属于消费者，先调用</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_del_all</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 一次性地将列表中的元素全部摘下，再进行遍历处理。从这个意义上看，</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">34</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p047_img01.png)
