## Page 48

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">该链表更多起到队列的作用。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中断分为上半部分和下半部分。上半部分会关闭所有中断，使系统失去响</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">应，为了减少失去响应的时间，上半部分不能休眠，复杂的操作也得放到下半部分</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">执行。这意味着上半部分的代码不能使用加锁操作，否则容易发生中断重入，所以</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">就又产生了加锁的需求。提高</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中断上半部分使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 数据结构能力的最好方式</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">是使用无锁</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，数据结构如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct llist_head { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct llist_node *first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct llist_node { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct llist_node *next; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">}; </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核实现的方法是使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cmpxchg</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cmpxchg</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏也是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Intel</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 平台的一个汇编指令，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">其作用是让读取、比较、改变这三个操作都是原子的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cmpxchg</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏有</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 个参数，如</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">果第一个参数和第二个参数相等，则将第三个参数写入第一个参数指向的地址。如</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">果第一个参数和第二个参数不相等，则返回第三个参数，本意是将第三个参数写入</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">第一个参数指向的地址，所以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cmpxchg</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 宏先读出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">head-&gt;next</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">head-&gt;first</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 作为第</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">一个参数，紧接着读出的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">head-&gt;first</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 作为第二个参数，要添加的新节点作为第三个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">参数，代码如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">bool llist_add_batch(struct llist_node *new_first, struct llist_node </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*new_last,struct llist_head *head) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct llist_node *first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">do { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">new_last-&gt;next = first = ACCESS_ONCE(head-&gt;first); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} while (cmpxchg(&amp;head-&gt;first, first, new_first) != first); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return !first; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static inline bool llist_add(struct llist_node *new, struct llist_head </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">*head) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return llist_add_batch(new, new, head); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">35</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 49

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在调度系统中，每一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 都会有一个运行队列叫</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct rq</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，当前</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的任务</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">调度的信息大都存储在这个结构体中。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct rq</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中，有一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct llist_head </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">wake_list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 域，这个域是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的无锁单链表，其作用是接受其他的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 核心送过来的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">任务，并且在本</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 可以调度的时候进行调度执行，这个机制整体上叫作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ttwu</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">try </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">to wake up</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）。下面是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ttwu</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的一个函数的代码。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">static void ttwu_queue_remote(struct task_struct *p, int cpu, int </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">wake_flags) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct rq *rq = cpu_rq(cpu); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">p-&gt;sched_remote_wakeup = !!(wake_flags &amp; WF_MIGRATED); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (llist_add(&amp;p-&gt;wake_entry, &amp;cpu_rq(cpu)-&gt;wake_list)) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (!set_nr_if_polling(rq-&gt;idle)) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">smp_send_reschedule(cpu); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">else </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">trace_sched_wake_idle_without_ipi(cpu); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">void sched_ttwu_pending(void) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">{ </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct rq *rq = this_rq(); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct llist_node *llist = llist_del_all(&amp;rq-&gt;wake_list); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct task_struct *p, *t; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">struct rq_flags rf; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">if (!llist) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">return; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">rq_lock_irqsave(rq, &amp;rf); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">update_rq_clock(rq); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">llist_for_each_entry_safe(p, t, llist, wake_entry) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">ttwu_do_activate(rq, p, p-&gt;sched_remote_wakeup ? WF_MIGRATED : </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">0, &amp;rf); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">36</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p049_img01.png)

## Page 50

<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">rq_unlock_irqrestore(rq, &amp;rf); </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNew';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">} </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 认为自己没有足够的精力处理一个任务的时候，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ttwu_queue_remote</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">函数就唤醒一个相对空闲的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来代替它进行处理。这种唤醒另外一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 来处</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">理问题的操作是通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IPI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Inter Process Interrupt</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，核间中断）进行的。从一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">插入另外一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的唤醒队列的方式是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ttwu_queue_remote</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 函数，即无锁地将一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">任务插入另外一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 运行队列的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">wake_llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中，然后通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IPI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 唤醒目标</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">当目标</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 被唤醒的时候会检查自己运行队列的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">wake_llist</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct rq *rq = </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">this_rq()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">得到自己的运行队列，然后将运行队列中</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">wake_list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的所有任务都一次性摘</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">下：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct llist_node *llist = llist_del_all(&amp;rq-&gt;wake_list)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。这一步就是将无锁链表的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">多消费者全部摘取。在将无锁链表的多消费者全部摘取之后，</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">llist_for_each_entry_safe(p, t, llist, wake_entry)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">对已经摘下来的链表进行遍历，带有</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">safe</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 后缀的遍历函数则代表在遍历的过程中其可以被删除。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.3.2  </span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">树与</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">IDR </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">树是管理大型复杂结构最常用的数据结构类型。在内核中比较常见的是用于内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">存线性地址空间管理的红黑树（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">rbtree</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）和用于文件系统文件组织的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B+</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">树（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">btree</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）（一</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">些文件系统也会实现自己的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B+</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">树），以及用于组建整数查找的基树（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">radix tree</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">基树与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">trie</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 树非常类似，只是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 基树一般用来定位整数，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">trie</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 树一般用来定位字</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">符串。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IDR</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Integer ID Management</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）机制在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核中指的是整数</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ID</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 管理机制，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">大部分需要申请释放整数资源的操作，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核中最终都会转换为对一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IDR</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">组件的使用。在常见的硬件驱动中，由于设备地址和设备编号一直都是强对应的关</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">系，所以对设备编号和设备地址的处理属于同一类问题。当需要从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">PID</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 找到对应的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">进程结构体时，可以向</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IDR</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 输入</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">PID</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，以快速得到对应的结构体指针，这就是一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">ID</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 值快速搜索得到对应的结构体指针的需求。搜索的频率总是高的，所以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IDR</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">会采用搜索树，也就是被优化过的基树。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">trie</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 树是数据结构中常见的字典树，常被用于搜索字符串。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 基树是一种压</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">缩的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">trie</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 树，简单说就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">trie</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 树中只有一个子节点被压缩成一个单独的节点。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

## Page 51

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">最新的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 内核在实现基树的时候，只保留了原来基树的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Matthew Wilcox</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">设计了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 上刻意与原来的基树保持类似的设计，使得基树的应用可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">很容易就过渡到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">。之所以要设计</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，有很大一部分原因是基树的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 设</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">计不能让人满意，因此</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 通过观察已有的类似的使用方式，提供了一个新的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">设计方式：一套是简单的基础</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，在内部自动进行了锁和内存管理；另外一套是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">高级的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，可以深入到数据结构体的内部。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">IDR</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 直接使用基树，但是基树的实现</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">已经变成了使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的封装。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 相当于一个树形数组，从外部看，这是一个可以容纳</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">64</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 位整数的数组，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">其实现并不是真的使用一个大数组，而是在内部组织了层次的结构，当需要用到对</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">应数的时候，才会产生该数所对应的内部树的节点。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:13.98pt;color:#000000">2.3.3  xarray </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">．</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对比红黑树与哈希表</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是内核比较新的用于取代基树的数据结构，也叫作动态数组，从本质上</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">来看，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 延续了基树的思路并对基树进行了改良。基树以前存在的主要问题</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">如下。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）内核的基树在本质上是一个动态数组，但是并不是一棵树，所以其对应的</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 对使用者不是很友好。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）基树的实现需要用户进行锁处理。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">新的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 增加了默认的锁处理，并且提供了高级</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，使得用户可以更好地</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">控制锁的行为。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内核面临的一个大问题是对内存页的管理。每个进程所有映射的页面都需要被</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">划分成很多个内存块，有的内存块是文件映射，有的内存块是内存映射和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">brk</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">，这些</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内存空间并不一定是连续的。在大部分情况下，在进程可见的地址空间内，每个内</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">存块都被组成一棵红黑树，树中的每个节点都有开始和结束的内存位置。当需要申</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">请一个新的映射的时候，就可以从这棵树中快速找到可用的位置，或者当操作一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">内存位置的时候，可以快速找到这个内存位置属于什么映射。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">整个过程都需要一个能够管理内存不规则使用且又需要快速查找的数据结构。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">类似的需求还有用于管理文件在内存中缓存的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">address_space</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 中的页，该需求使用基</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">38</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p051_img01.png)



![](./200600-深入Linux内核架构与底层原理（第2版）-ISBN：978-7-121-43689-5_assets/images/p051_img02.png)

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 52

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">树来组织，因为有的文件内容需要映射缓存，有的则不需要，是否需要映射缓存在</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">本质上是由用户的使用情况决定的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的文件缓存是基于文件块序号的，而进程的内存映射是由连续内存块组成</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">entry</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 管理的，管理的粒度是不一样的，这也反映出红黑树与基树在使用选型上的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">区别。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">对于内存空间的内存映射这种功能，从内存资源占用上来看，最适合选择按照</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">节点为管理单位的红黑树的方式。而对文件缓存（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">page cache</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">）的管理最适合选择以</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">基树为单位的管理方式。这两种管理方式在单核查找性能上类似，但是如果数据稀</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">疏，基树的内存浪费就会远大于以节点为管理单位的红黑树，反之，如果数据比较</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">密集，红黑树的管理成本就会很高。这两者还有一个巨大的区别，就是在多核性能</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">上，红黑树的操作需要对整棵树加锁，涉及变色与旋转，一个节点的改变可能会带</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">来父节点、子节点和兄弟节点的同步变动。而基树由于具有从上而下的确定性，完</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">全没有变色选择这种操作，在并发上可以做到很轻量级的锁。在内核中直接使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">RCU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 锁。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">在使用方式上，红黑树的节点可以嵌入其他数据结构，而基树的节点不可以嵌</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">入其他数据结构，只可以由基树直接保存整数或者由指针来指向其他数据结构。这</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">种使用上的区别就决定了使用基树的场景必定是相对独立的功能模块，这与内核中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的大部分数据结构可以灵活地嵌入其他数据结构中的做法有区别。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">像基树和红黑树这种用来加速查找的数据结构，链表是比较早期被选择用于解</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">决这个需求问题的，因为链表具有简单性，其在早期比较容易验证想法，然后就是</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">红黑树。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 旨在对使用者提供一个类似动态数组的使用体验。哈希表的性能是极高</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的，但是缺陷也很明显，因为元素之间没有顺序性，或者说无法按照特定的顺序进</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">行元素定位。要同时做到可遍历和高效查找，一般需要在哈希表之外同步维护一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">外部的链表或其他有序数据结构，这样可以综合哈希表的定位性能和外部数据结构</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">的顺序能力。但是这仍然无法解决顺序元素之间的离散问题，当遍历顺序元素的时</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">候，通常希望顺序元素都尽可能地落在同一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cache</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 行中，以得到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">cache</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 加速的优势，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">但是链表和红黑树等顺序数据结构并不具备该能力。在文件系统上广泛使用的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B+</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">树具备这种连续性能力，但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">B+</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">树在提高</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 效率上比红黑树差很多，只适合使</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">用在层次敏感的查找场景。这并不是说哈希表相比</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 就一无是处，布谷鸟哈希</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">表出色的内存稳定占用的表现就是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 不具备的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">第2 章 系统结构 </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">39</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> </span>

電子工業出版社
PUBLISHING HOUSE OF ELECTRONICS INDUSTRY

## Page 53

<span style="font-family:'FZZDXJW--GB1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">深入Linux 内核架构与底层原理（第2 版） </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">可以说，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 是哈希函数固定的多级哈希表，最适用的场景是整数域。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">继承了多级哈希的节约空间、快速索引、局部锁的高性能特性。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">．</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的主要数据结构</span><span style="font-family:'Arial';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的整体结构图如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">2-4</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 所示。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">xarray</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000"> 的整体数据结构是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRoman';font-size:10.50pt;color:#000000">struct xarray</span>
